</a><span class="white-space-pre"> </span>di registrazione richiede una significativa manodopera e una buona dose di burocrazia a cui dare seguito. Numeri? Nell'<!----><a href="/feed/hashtag/ue/" id="ember258" class="ember-view">      <span class="visually-hidden">hashtag</span>
      <span><span aria-hidden="true">#</span>UE</span>
</a><!---->, le istituzioni finanziarie tradizionali attualmente spendono oltre 100 miliardi di euro per la conformità<span class="white-space-pre"> </span><a href="/feed/hashtag/kyc/" id="ember259" class="ember-view">      <span class="visually-hidden">hashtag</span>
      <span><span aria-hidden="true">#</span>KYC</span>
</a><!---->.<!----><br><br><!---->Secondo CypherTrace, più della metà degli scambi di<span class="white-space-pre"> </span><a href="/feed/hashtag/criptovalute/" id="ember260" class="ember-view">      <span class="visually-hidden">hashtag</span>
      <span><span aria-hidden="true">#</span>criptovalute</span>
</a><span class="white-space-pre"> </span>non ha seguito alcun regolamento KYC al 2020 e più di 3 miliardi di dollari sono stati riciclati attraverso transazioni di cripto nel 2019.<!----><br><br><!---->Ora, ciò che sorprende è che la maggior parte di questi scambi ha interessato proprio l’Europa, ovvero un’area geografica in cui ci sono severe normative finanziarie e dove gli aggiornamenti della direttiva antiriciclaggio (AMLD) hanno apportato ulteriori restringimenti rispetto alle regole KYC.<!----><br><br><!---->Sinceramente, questi aggiornamenti impallidiscono di fronte alla portata delle normative AML-KYC sui fornitori di servizi di asset virtuali (VASP) che vigono negli States.<!----><br><br><!---->Ma in questo quadro, quello che sfugge ai più è che compliance,<span class="white-space-pre"> </span><a href="/feed/hashtag/responsabilit%C3%A0/" id="ember261" class="ember-view">      <span class="visually-hidden">hashtag</span>
      <span><span aria-hidden="true">#</span>responsabilità</span>
</a><span class="white-space-pre"> </span>e<span class="white-space-pre"> </span><a href="/feed/hashtag/sostenibilit%C3%A0/" id="ember262" class="ember-view">      <span class="visually-hidden">hashtag</span>
      <span><span aria-hidden="true">#</span>sostenibilità</span>
</a><span class="white-space-pre"> </span>sono concetti connessi, tutte le società sono chiamate a mappare le norme di riferimento a cui devono conformarsi nel proprio operato e non siamo assolutamente di fronte ad uno sforzo estemporaneo, ma ad un impegno per garantire continuità.<span class="white-space-pre"> </span><br><br><!---->La compliance, certo, deve essere essa stessa sostenibile. Tuttavia, la compliance è un investimento non solo un dovere.<span class="white-space-pre"> </span><br><br><!---->Il concetto stesso di compliance non si esaurisce nel rispetto della legge ma si esprime attraverso l’adozione di comportamenti virtuosi e il supporto di partner altrettanto virtuosi che intendono perseguire obiettivi di sostenibilità condivisi nel rispetto di clienti, fornitori e<span class="white-space-pre"> </span><a href="/feed/hashtag/stakeholders/" id="ember263" class="ember-view">      <span class="visually-hidden">hashtag</span>
      <span><span aria-hidden="true">#</span>stakeholders</span>
</a><!---->, i quali nel compiere le loro scelte di adesione ad una progettualità o ad un servizio come utenti, ormai tendono a valutare più il contesto nel quale quel servizio viene generato che il servizio in sè.<!----><br><br><!---->Bisogna fare pace con se stessi: se vogliamo che le<span class="white-space-pre"> </span><a href="/feed/hashtag/crypto/" id="ember264" class="ember-view">      <span class="visually-hidden">hashtag</span>
      <span><span aria-hidden="true">#</span>crypto</span>
</a><span class="white-space-pre"> </span>siano adottate in massa (avverrà davvero ?) bisogna passare per la "via crucis" della regolamentazione fatta di molte decisioni che nei prossimi mesi non condivideremo; se riteniamo che<span class="white-space-pre"> </span><a href="/feed/hashtag/bitcoin/" id="ember265" class="ember-view">      <span class="visually-hidden">hashtag</span>
      <span><span aria-hidden="true">#</span>bitcoin</span>
</a><span class="white-space-pre"> </span>e figlie debbano restare nello spazio parzialmente anarchico che le ha generate è troppo tardi e comodo, le crypto avrebbero dovuto restare nelle mani di pochi incauti investitori.<!----><br><br><!---->C'è bisogno di meno polemiche e lamentele e di un impegno collettivo, di dialogo col regolatore per rendere chiaro che le crypto rappresentano un'opportunità di crescita per il Paese e sono qui per restare.<!----><br><br><a href="/feed/hashtag/blockchaintechnology/" id="ember266" class="ember-view">      <span class="visually-hidden">hashtag</span>
      <span><span aria-hidden="true">#</span>blockchaintechnology</span>
</a></span>

      <span class="inline-show-more-text__link-container-collapsed">
<!---->        <button class="inline-show-more-text__button
            inline-show-more-text__button--light
            link" aria-expanded="false" type="button">
          …show more
        </button>
      </span>

                      <div class="pv2">

      inline-flex justify-center align-self-flex-start
      
      " target="_blank" href="https://www.ibno.eu/downloads/donne-e-industria-blockchain-indagine-sulle-carriere-professionali-e-loccupazione-femminile-in-italia-e-in-europa/">

      </span>
  </a>

        <li class="pvs-list__item--with-top-padding ">
                <div class="display-flex ">
    <div class="display-flex full-width">
    
      
  <div class="pv-shared-text-with-see-more t-14 t-normal t-black display-flex align-items-center">
    <div class="inline-show-more-text
    inline-show-more-text--is-collapsed
    
    
    
    " style="line-height:1.9rem;max-height:3.8rem;">

    <span aria-hidden="true"><!---->This deep analysis moves from the partnership between the #Blockchain Observatory (IBNO) of the University of Naples Federico II and the international community Blockchain Ladies.<!----><br><!---->Topical issues are deepened and described: how Blockchain is influencing the career of lawyers; policies that incentivize women and #girls in accessing #ICT professional roles; #paygap; the role of Blockchain as a stimulus for the next generation of women entrepreneurs; #fintech; #mining; #NFTs; the relationship between women and crypto-journalism; the role of the Blockchain Technology in the workplace as a tool to prevent and counter abuse.<!----><br><!---->Establishing programs to incentivize women to pursue careers in this area is crucial, the study aimed to better analyze the issue in order to increasingly refine actionable strategies. The report offers an overview of some factors that characterize the gender gap in order to offer targeted solutions and reduce the negative effects of the phenomenon.<!----><br><!---->A phenomenon that is above all socio-economic and that requires effective interventions, subject to quality control for continuous improvement and a rigorous comparison between the benefits and possible effects of overcoming the #genderissue in #technology.<!----></span><span class="visually-hidden"><!---->This deep analysis moves from the partnership between the #Blockchain Observatory (IBNO) of the University of Naples Federico II and the international community Blockchain Ladies.
Topical issues are deepened and described: how Blockchain is influencing the career of lawyers; policies that incentivize women and #girls in accessing #ICT professional roles; #paygap; the role of Blockchain as a stimulus for the next generation of women entrepreneurs; #fintech; #mining; #NFTs; the relationship between women and crypto-journalism; the role of the Blockchain Technology in the workplace as a tool to prevent and counter abuse.
Establishing programs to incentivize women to pursue careers in this area is crucial, the study aimed to better analyze the issue in order to increasingly refine actionable strategies. The report offers an overview of some factors that characterize the gender gap in order to offer targeted solutions and reduce the negative effects of the phenomenon.
A phenomenon that is above all socio-economic and that requires effective interventions, subject to quality control for continuous improvement and a rigorous comparison between the benefits and possible effects of overcoming the #genderissue in #technology.<!----></span>

    <div class="inline-show-more-text

    " style="line-height:1.9rem;max-height:3.8rem;">

    <span aria-hidden="true"><!---->Abstract<!----><br><br><!---->Cadmium (Cd) is a transition metal belonging to group IIB of the periodic table. Cd affects the activity of ion channels and membrane transporters and induces oxidative stress ultimately leading to mitochondrial damage and cell apoptosis. It also causes autophagy that reduces cell damage. Cd interferes with DNA repair systems and affects epigenetic control mechanisms, mainly DNA methylation. Cd is an important toxicant. Acute intoxication usually occurs in professionally exposed people working in factories processing this metal, whereas chronic toxicity may be the consequence of inapparent Cd exposure through tobacco smoking or the ingestion of contaminated food. Inapparent Cd exposure is emerging as an important cause of chronic kidney disease and osteoporosis.<!----></span><span class="visually-hidden"><!---->Abstract

Cadmium (Cd) is a transition metal belonging to group IIB of the periodic table. Cd affects the activity of ion channels and membrane transporters and induces oxidative stress ultimately leading to mitochondrial damage and cell apoptosis. It also causes autophagy that reduces cell damage. Cd interferes with DNA repair systems and affects epigenetic control mechanisms, mainly DNA methylation. Cd is an important toxicant. Acute intoxication usually occurs in professionally exposed people working in factories processing this metal, whereas chronic toxicity may be the consequence of inapparent Cd exposure through tobacco smoking or the ingestion of contaminated food. Inapparent Cd exposure is emerging as an important cause of chronic kidney disease and osteoporosis.<!----></span>
